e
 next August
 esbiai kii home lone or auto lone bazaar main kramash: 35 fisadi or 36 fisadi kii hissedari he
 After continuous appeals, the Reserve Bank of India (RBI) recently directed banks to link all loan repo rates
 RBI ne sabhi bainkon ko 1 oktober se repo rate ke saath home lone, auto lone, personal lone or emsamai sector ke sabhi prakaar ke lone ko jodne ke liye kaha he
 In fact, for the past few months, the central bank has been continuously asking all government and private banks to link bank loans with repo rates
 lekin kai bank RBI kii apil ko nanandaaj kar rahe the
 After which the central bank has to give instructions with the deadline
 iske alaava arabiai ne repo jaise bahari benchmark ke tahat byaaj daron main 3 maheene main kam se kam ek baar badlaav karne ko kaha he

 film main anupam kher (anupam Kher) purv pradhanmantri manmohan singh (manmohan Singh) bane hai to akshay khanna (akshaye Khanna) ne sanjay baru (sanjay Baru) kaa kirdaar nibhaayaa he
 The entire film revolves around these two
 'da accidental prime ministar (the Accidental Prime Minister)' jaldbaaji main banaai gai film lagati he, or film main kai ditels main bhi diarector chookte najar aate hai
 In the film, Manmohan calls Sanjay Baru his own Sanjay
 is tarah manmohan singh kii jindagi kii mahabharat ko sanjay kii najaron se dekhne kaa mauka miltaa he
 'the Accidental Prime Minister' begins in 2004 with Sonia Gandhi stepping down as Prime Minister and then Manmohan Singh being made the Prime Minister
 iske baad jarnlist sanjay baru kii entry hoti he or manmohan singh ke chahete hone kii vajah se ve unke media adwiser ban jate hai

 is tarah film puri tarah se sanjay baru (sanjay Baru) ke kandhe par savaar hokar chalati he, or film ke hero manmohan singh (manmohan Singh) nahin balki sanjay baru hai
 Sanjay Baru wants everything according to his own and sometimes in the film it seems that he wants to run the PMO
 kai maukon par ve media adwiser se aage ke kaam karte bhi dikhte hai

 lekin unke bolne kaa andaaj kai baar hansi laa detaa he or phir kai maukon par unki chaal bhi khatkati he

 ye baat khatkati he

 ye thodaa thik nahin lagata

 kul milakar film main sab sayaane the, sirf manmohan hi nadaan the

 ise surya saptami, rath aarogy saptami, suryarath saptami, putr saptami aadi naamon se bhi janaa jaataa he

 'ola ke upaadhyaksh (marketing) sudarshan gangrade ne kaha, 'is saajhedaari kaa hamaara uddeshy bharat ke saat shaharon, dilli / ensiaar, mumbai, pune, bengaluru, hyderabad, kolkata or ahmedabad main apane upabhoktaaon or smartphone kharidne kii ichha rakhane vaale logon ko aath disambar se is seva kaa laabh pradaan karnaa he

 Kashmiri Attacked in Lucknow: Two vendors of Kashmir who were selling dry fruits on a crowded street in Uttar Pradesh capital Lucknow were attacked and beaten with slaps and sticks on Wednesday by people belonging to a right-wing organization
 itnaa hi nahin, rhite wing sanghathan se jude hamalaavaron ne done kashmiri ke saath marpet kaa video bhi saajha kiya
 However, with the help of the local people, both the Kashmiri youth were rescued from the clutches of the attackers
 bhagavadhari gundon ne jin do kashmiriyon ko peeta he unamem se ek kaa naam afjal nike he or duusare kaa abdul salaam

 darasal, yah ghatana buudhvaar shaam 5 baje hui
